 First Hardoi Farrukhabad falls in the Northern Parliamentary constituency
 1952 main chunaav main bulaaki ram verma saansad chune gaye the
 After this, Hardoi became Lok Sabha seat in 1957
 congress 6 baar yahaan se chunaav jeetne main safal rahi, jabaki 3-3 baar bijepi or sapa is seat par jeet kaa paracham laharaa chuki hai
 In the Lok Sabha elections in 1957, the Jana Sangh managed to win the Hardoi seat, but in the 1957 by-election, the Congress captured this seat
 iske baad se 1977 main congress ke haathon se ye seat nikali, lekin 1980 or 1984 main phir jeet kaa paracham laharaaya
 In 1989 Lok Sabha elections, Paramai Lal of Janata Dal won from here and reached Parliament
 iske baad ram mandir andolan ke dauraan 1991 main hue loksabhaa chunaav main bijepi ne is seat par kabja jamaaya or lagaataar do baar jai prakaash yahaan se saansad chune gaye, lekin 1998 main usha verma ne sapa ummidavaar ke taur par utarkar bijepi ke jeet kaa silsile ko roak diya

 arun ko bhi dilli se bulaayaa ja rahaa he
 Former Indian captain and former chief selector Dilip Vengsarkar believes that the Indian cricketer succumbed to complacency after a recent good performance and this is the main reason for the team's poor performance in the current Test series against England
 vengsarakar kaa saath hi maananaa he ki team ko england kii majboot team ke khilaaf taiyaari karne kaa behad kam samay mila
 Important pieces of Vengsarkar's interview went to England to watch the first two Tests of the series
 prashn: kya aapane bhartiya team ke itane kharaab pradarshan kii ummid kii thi
 What is the reason for the poor performance of the team that won the World Cup title just four months ago
 vengsarakar: eemaandaaree se kahuun to mujhe pataa tha ki yah bharat ke liye mushkil shrinkhalaa hone vaali he kyonki unhen ek majboot team kaa saamana karnaa tha jo lay main he or haal ke samay main lagaataar acha pradarshan kar rahi thi
 Apart from this, their bowling attack was better and as a team they got plenty of time to prepare for the series
 duusari taraf bharat westeindies main vyast shrinkhalaa khilne ke baad pahunchaa or unhen england kii paristhitiyon ke mutabik taiyaari karne or lay main aane kaa kaaphi kam samay mila
 i think India fell prey to complacency after a good performance in the last few seasons
 prashn: kya aapako lagata he ki ek gendbaaj jahir khan par adhik nirbharta team ke liye acchhee nahin he
 Answer: Are there any other options? We have to accept that we do not have much choice in batting or bowling, especially when we face a strong opponent
 ham parakhe hue khilaadiyon par nirbhar hai phir bhale hi ve chot ke baad vaapasi kar rahe hon or unhen adhik match abhyaas nahin ho
 You cannot compete like this
 adhik khilaadi sahaj sthiti main hai or unhen acchhee tarah pataa he ki sheersh str par unke liye pratispardhaa nahin he
 Question: Where did the team have trouble in England
 kya lords test se pehle use or a5yaas match khilne chahie the
 Answer: When the team is going out of Asia, it is very important that they get enough match practice to adjust to the conditions before the first Test match
 westeindies se lekar england tak halaat kaaphi alag hai
 The first Test of the series determines the fate of the losing team most of the time in the series
 isse team kaa manobal girtaa he or asaadhaaran pradarshan kiye bina isse nahin ubra ja saktaa
 Question: Were you happy with Dhoni's captaincy while you were there
 yaa aapako laga ki kshetrarakshakon ko lekar vah behatar kar saktaa tha
 Answer: What can the captain do when the main bowler is suffering from injuries and important catches are being dripped
 usne lords main apane wicketcaping gloves chhodkar gendbaaji karke yah spasht kar diya tha

 sachin tendulkar ne bhi apane str kii jhalak dikhaai

 uttar: beshak
 The job of the selectors is to identify and refine the talent
 unhen bhavishya kii yojana dikhaani chahie

 samasya yaheen par he

 jab tak aap jeet rahe hon tab tak sab kuch thik he lekin kisi bhi nattejey ke liye taiyaar rahanaa chahie

 These committees had to solve the staff problem in four months but so far seven months have passed
 ab khabar he ki sarkaar kii ore se banaai kai teen samitiyon main se ek jiske paas alouns kaa mudda bhi tha ne apni report ko antim praaroop de diya he or jald hi yah samiti apni report vittamantralay ko saunp degi

 ullekhneey he ki centre sarkaar ke kai vibhaagon ke karmchaaree is baat se kaaphi naaraaz chal rahe hai ki sarkaar kii ore se karmchaaree kii maangon kii ore dhyaan nahin diya ja rahaa he

 jis report ko sarkaar ko chaar maheene main de diya janaa chahie tha vah report abhi tak nahin taiyaar he

 kendriya karmchaariyon kaa maananaa he ki badha hua bhatta dene se sarkari khajaane par kuch atirikt boj aayega isliye sarkaar in maamalon main deree kar rahi he
 (7th pay commission: shock to central employees, changes in allowance will be applicable from March 2017!) kai karmchaaree sanghon ke netaaon kaa kahana he ki sarkaar ne saatven vetan ayog ke vivaadit muddon par charchaa ke liye kai samitiyon kaa gathan kar diya he
 These committees discussed the Pay Commission report, but nothing positive has come to light yet
 abhi tak in samitiyon se ek bhi aisa nirnay saamne nahin aayaa he jisase kendriya karmchaaree santusht hon
 (staff angry over PM Narendra Modi's 'surgical strike' in railway-defense sector, strike announced on 16 March) ab kendriya karmchaariyon ko yah bhi ashanka sata rahi he ki jis alouns ko sarkaar ko pichley saal july maah se diya janaa chahie tha ab vah nae saal main milenge to karmchaariyon ko pichley kai maheenon kaa bade hue alouns ke na milane se kaaphi nuksaan hoga

 is dauraan narendra modi sabhi netaaon kaa abhibhavadan kar rahe the

 darasal keshubhai patel ko pradhanmantri narendra modi apana rajnatik guru maanate hai

 keshubhai ne 2012 main apni khud kii gujarat parivartan party banaai thi or chunaav bhi lade the

 jiske kuch vakt ke andar hi keshubhai ne apni gujarat parivartan party ko bijepi main marz kar diya tha

 india today anti phek news war room (AFWA) ne modi ke chote bhai prahlada modi se is bare main baat kii or unhone hamen bataaya artical main likhi baaten saraasar jhooth hai
 His family never lodged an FIR against Modi
 is artical main koi 'dilli news network' kii biline di gai he
 We did not find any media house with this name nor did we get any mention of such news in any news report about Modi
 agar is artical par gaur kiya jaae to isamen bhashaa kii bhi kaaphi galtiyaan hai jo kii pradhanmantri modi par likhe artical main hona mushkil he
 It can be understood that this article is fake
 modi ne shanivaar ko ek raily main purv pradhanmantri or rahul gandhi ke pita rajeev gandhi ko lekar ek bayaan main kaha tha ki unka jivan 'bhrashtachari number van' netaa ke rup main khatm hua he
